          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Linktera | Transform Your Future

Founded in 2011 in Istanbul, Linktera is a technology consultancy company that delivers end-to-end solutions in consulting, system integration, project management, and product development primarily for leading institutions in the finance sector. With a team of over 300 experts, Linktera brings deep expertise in financial technologies, risk management, regulatory reporting, robotic process automation (RPA), data analytics, artificial intelligence, and digital transformation.

Through its innovation hub, Linktera Labs, the company develops products tailored to accelerate digital transformation and address the unique needs of the financial industry. Solutions such as SpineX, Payify, BRM, CreditBoost, RateLink, and DAT offer value across a wide range of functions-from treasury management and credit scoring to financial consolidation and regulatory compliance-demonstrating Linkteraâ€™s commitment to sector-specific innovation.

Leveraging strategic partnerships with leading global technology providers such as SAS, UiPath, Murex and Druid, Linktera delivers world-class automation and AI-driven solutions. These collaborations enhance the value delivered to clients and strengthen Linkteraâ€™s global capabilities and technological excellence.

With a strong focus on capability building, Linktera Talent Factory offers structured training, real-world project experience, and mentorship through programs like CodeFactory, TestFactory, and Talent Hub creating a steady pipeline of industry-ready talent. As a reflection of Linkteraâ€™s Smart Sourcing expertise, it helps organizations optimize processes, access the right talent, and drive sustainable success with tailored solutions.



Headquartered in Istanbul, Linktera extends its global reach with Linktera Robotics in San Jose, Linktera Middle East FZE in Dubai, and additional offices in Switzerland and Qatar continuing to provide innovative and sustainable solutions across markets.
